[?1049h[?1h=#===============================================================================
# ARBITER
#===============================================================================
# Description: The Arbiter is responsible for:
# - Loading, manipulating and dispatching the configuration
# - Validating the health of all other Shinken daemons
# - Issuing global directives to Shinken daemons (kill, activate-spare, etc.)
# https://shinken.readthedocs.org/en/latest/08_configobjects/arbiter.html
#===============================================================================
# IMPORTANT: If you use several arbiters you MUST set the host_name on each
# servers to its real DNS name ('hostname' command).
#===============================================================================
define arbiter {
    arbiter_name    arbiter-master
    #host_name       node1       ; CHANGE THIS if you have several Arbiters (like with a spare)
    address         localhost   ; DNS name or IP
    port            7770
    spare           0           ; 1 = is a spare, 0 = is not a spare

    ## Interesting modules:
    # - named-pipe               = Open the named pipe nagios.cmd
    # - mongodb                  = Load hosts from a mongodb database
    # - pickle-retention-arbiter = Save data before exiting
    # - nsca                     = NSCA server
    # - vmware-auto-linking      = Lookup at Vphere server for dependencies
    # - import-glpi              = Import configuration from GLPI (need plugin monitoring for GLPI in server side)
    # - tsca                     = TSCA server
    # - mysql-mport              = Load configuration from a MySQL database
    # - ws-arbiter               = WebService for pushing results to the arbiter
    # - collectd                 = Receive collectd perfdata
    # - snmp-booster             = Snmp bulk polling module, configuration linker
    # - import-landscape         = Import hosts from Landscape (Ubuntu/Canonical management tool)
    # - aws                     = Import hosts from Amazon AWS (here EC2)
    # - ip-tag                  = Tag a host based on it's IP range
    # - file-tag                        = Tag a host if it's on a flat file
    # - csv-tag                 = Tag a host from the content of a CSV file
    
    modules      
    
    # Enable https or not
    use_ssl               0
    # enable certificate/hostname check, will avoid man in the middle attacks

[1mNAME[0m[m
       shinken-receiver - Shinken receiver daemon[m

[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       Shinken receiver daemon[m
[m

       dispatch data.[m

[3;1H[1mNAME[0m[m
[4;1H       shinken-receiver - Shinken receiver daemon[m
[5;1H[m
[6;1H[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
[7;1H       shinken-receiver [[4moptions[24m] ...[m
[8;1H[m
[9;1H[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
[10;1H       Shinken receiver daemon[m
[11;1H[m
[12;1H       The  shinken-receiver  daemon  manages passive information and serves as a buffer that will be read from by the shinken-arbiter to[m
[13;1H       dispatch data.[m
[14;1H[m
[15;1H[1mOPTIONS[0m[m
[16;1H       [1m--version[0m[m

[23;1H              Run in daemon mode.[m
[24;1H[m
[25;1H       [1m-r,[0m [1m--replace[0m[m
[26;1H              Replace previous running arbiter.[m
[27;1H[m

[?1049h[?1h=shinken(8)                                               System Manager's Manual                                               shinken(8)[m
[m
[1mNAME[0m[m
       shinken - Shinken packs and modules manager[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       shinken [OPTION]... [4mFILE[24m[m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       Shinken packs and modules manager[m
[m
       Shinken  is  a  usefull  tool  to  manage  your  Shinken  packs  and  modules  and  can be used to download packs and modules from[m
       [4mhttp://shinken.io[24m and also to publish yours.[m
[m
[1mOPTIONS[0m[m
       [1m--version[0m[m
              Show version number and exit[m
[m
       [1m-A[0m [4mAPI_KEY[24m[1m,[0m [1m--api-keys[0m [4mAPI_KEY[24m[m
              Your API key for uploading the package to the Shinken.io website. If you don't have one, please go to your account page[m
[m
       [1m-l,[0m [1m--list[0m[m
              List available commands[m
[m
       [1m--init[0m Initialize/refill your shinken.ini file (default home directory)[m
[m
       [1m-D[0m     Enable the debug mode[m
[m
       [1m-c[0m [4mINICONFIG[24m[1m,[0m [1m--config[0m [4mINICONFIG[24m[m
              Path to your shinken.ini file.[m
[m
       [1m-h,[0m [1m--help[0m[m
              Print detailed help screen.[m
[m
[1mAUTHORS[0m[m
       David Hannequin.  Michael Leinartas.[m
[m

Ce plugin v√©rifie la place utilis√© sur un syst√®me de fichier mont√©
et g√©n√®re une alerte si la place disponible est plus petite qu'un des seuils fourni


Utilisation:
 check_disk -w limit -c limit [-W limit] [-K limit] {-p path | -x device}
[-C] [-E] [-e] [-f] [-g group ] [-k] [-l] [-M] [-m] {-A | [-R path] [-r path]}
[-s] [-t timeout] [-u unit] [-v] [-X type] [-N type] [-n]

Options:
 -h, --help
    Afficher l'aide d√©taill√©e
 -V, --version
    Afficher les informations relative √† la version
 --extra-opts=[section][@file]
    Read options from an ini file. See
    https://www.nagios-plugins.org/doc/extra-opts.html
    for usage and examples.
 -w, --warning=INTEGER
    Sortir avec un r√©sultat AVERTISSEMENT si moins de X unit√©s de disques sont libres
 -w, --warning=PERCENT%
    Sortir avec un r√©sultat AVERTISSEMENT si moins de X pour-cent du disque est libre
 -c, --critical=INTEGER
    Sortir avec un r√©sultat CRITIQUE si moins de X unit√©s du disque sont libres
 -c, --critical=PERCENT%
    Exit with CRITICAL status if less than PERCENT of disk space is free
 -W, --iwarning=PERCENT%
    Sortir avec un r√©sultat AVERTISSEMENT si moins de X pour-cent des inodes sont libres
 -K, --icritical=PERCENT%
    Sortir avec un r√©sultat CRITIQUE si moins de X pour-cent des inodes sont libres
 -p, --path=PATH, --partition=PARTITION
    Mount point or block device as emitted by the mount(8) command (may be repeated)
 -x, --exclude_device=PATH <STRING>
    Ignorer le p√©riph√©rique (marche seulement lorsque -p est utilis√©)
 -C, --clear
    Effacer les seuils
 -E, --exact-match
    For paths or partitions specified with -p, only check for exact paths
 -e, --errors-only
    Afficher seulement les p√©riph√©riques/point de montage avec des erreurs
 -f, --freespace-ignore-reserved
    Don't account root-reserved blocks into freespace in perfdata
 -g, --group=NAME
    Group paths. Thresholds apply to (free-)space of all partitions together
 -k, --kilobytes
    Pareil √† '--units kB'
 -l, --local
    V√©rifier seulement les syst√®mes de fichiers locaux
 -L, --stat-remote-fs
    Only check local filesystems against thresholds. Yet call stat on remote filesystems
    to test if they are accessible (e.g. to detect Stale NFS Handles)
 -M, --mountpoint
    Afficher le point de montage au lieu de la partition
 -m, --megabytes
    Pareil √† '--units MB'
 -A, --all
    Explicitly select all paths. This is equivalent to -R '.*'
 -R, --eregi-path=PATH, --eregi-partition=PARTITION
    Expression rationnelle ind√©pendante de la case pour un r√©pertoire ou une partition (peut √™tre utilis√© plusieurs fois)
 -r, --ereg-path=PATH, --ereg-partition=PARTITION
    Expression rationnelle pour un r√©pertoire ou une partition (peut √™tre utilis√© plusieurs fois)
 -I, --ignore-eregi-path=PATH, --ignore-eregi-partition=PARTITION
    Expression rationnelle pour ignorer un r√©pertoire ou une partition (peut √™tre utilis√© plusieurs fois)
 -i, --ignore-ereg-path=PATH, --ignore-ereg-partition=PARTITION
    Expression rationnelle pour ignorer un r√©pertoire ou une partition (peut √™tre utilis√© plusieurs fois)
 -s, --show-status
    Show status for each path/partition
 -t, --timeout=INTEGER
    Seconds before plugin times out (default: 10)
 -u, --units=STRING
    Choisissez octets, kb, MB, GB, TB (par d√©faut: MB)
 -v, --verbose
    Affiche les informations de d√©boguage en ligne de commande (Nagios peut tronquer la sortie)
 -X, --exclude-type=TYPE
    Ignorer tout les syst√®mes de fichiers qui correspondent au type indiqu√© (peut √™tre utilis√© plusieurs fois)
 -N, --include-type=TYPE
    Check only filesystems of indicated type (may be repeated)
 -n, --newlines
    Multi-line output of each disk's status information on a new line

Exemples:
 check_disk -w 10% -c 5% -p /tmp -p /var -C -w 100000 -c 50000 -p /
    V√©rifie /tmp √† 10% et /var √† 5% et / √† 100MB et 50MB
 check_disk -w 100 -c 50 -C -w 1000 -c 500 -g sidDATA -r '^/oracle/SID/data.*$'
    Checks all filesystems not matching -r at 100M and 50M. The fs matching the -r regex
    are grouped which means the freespace thresholds are applied to all disks together
 check_disk -w 100 -c 50 -C -w 1000 -c 500 -p /foo -C -w 5% -c 3% -p /bar
    Checks /foo for 1000M/500M and /bar for 5/3%. All remaining volumes use 100M/50M
